<p>Almost all men own a set of shirts &ndash; right from students to working professionals. These garments are comfortable and versatile. Modern-day casual <a href="/men-shirts"class="seolink">shirts for men</a> have evolved from inner garments of medieval times. They were originally made of un-dyed, plain fabrics. Coloured shirts made an appearance around the 19th century. And by the 20th century, shirts became mainstream and accepted as outerwear of class.</p>
<p>At Myntra we are proud to host some of the best casual shirts for men online. You can choose from a wide range of options in fabrics, patterns, collar-type, sleeves and more.</p>
<p><strong>MEN&rsquo;S CASUAL SHIRTS AT MYNTRA: AN OPTION FOR EVERY OCCASION</strong></p>
<p>Look dapper and feel comfortable from within with our collection of the best <a href="/shop/men" class="seolink">men&rsquo;s</a> casual shirt brands. You can access the latest varieties and new casual shirts for men fresh from the fashion houses right here at Myntra.</p>
<p>Here is a look at a few types of casual shirts for men and how to create the perfect outfit for every occasion:</p>
<ol>
<li>Checked casual shirts for men are great for an outdoor adventure. Get yourself a buffalo-checked slim-fit shirt in the quintessential red and black combination. Wear it unbuttoned over a white round-neck <a href="/tshirts">T-shirt</a> along with charcoal grey trousers. Wear a brown <a href="/jackets" class="seolink">jacket</a> and a pair of rugged brown boots before you take a walk in the woods.</li>
<li>If you are planning to head to a beach-side resort, replace your T-shirts with casual shirts for men. Choose a cool blue shirt in solid and pair it up with red chino shorts. Go sock-free with a pair of beige lace-up shoes. Wear wayfarers and a gold cap for added style.</li>
<li>It is time to head for a night of weekend clubbing with striped casual shirts for men. Put on a black vertical-striped shirt with the sleeves folded at the elbows. Team it up with light blue distressed <a href="/jeans" class="seolink">jeans</a>. Brown leather shoes and a brown strap watch would complete the look.</li>
<li>For a dinner date, express your love and commitment with a crisp white shirt. Wear it with dark blue trousers with a striped pattern. Brown leather slip-on shoes would add more class to your outfit. Accessorise with a smart metallic watch and carry your cash or cards in a smooth wallet.</li>
<li>Shine on like a diamond dressed in silk shirts. Pick up a silk shirt in green, or off-white and wear it with our <a href="/dhotis" class="seolink">dhotis</a> for your local festivals. Alternatively, pick up a red or maroon shirt, and wear it inserted with trousers for parties.</li>
</ol>
<p>Check out other variations in casual shirts for men such as colour-blocked, micro-checks gingham checks, polka dots, horizontal stripes and more such patterns.</p>
